namespace = agot_nicknames

#Generic Nicknames
agot_nicknames.0100 = {
	type = character_event
	hidden = yes

	#Makes them important
	trigger = {
		has_any_nickname = no
		is_adult = yes
		OR = {
			prestige >= 500
			is_ruler = yes
			any_close_family_member = {
				is_ruler = yes
			}
			has_trait = kingsguard
			has_trait = education_martial_prowess_3
			has_trait = education_martial_prowess_4
			has_trait = education_martial_prowess_5
		}
	}
	option = {
		random_list = {
			1000 = {

			}
			50 = { #Heroic Nicknames
				trigger = {
					prowess >= 25
					ai_boldness >= medium_positive_boldness
				}
				random_list = {
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_warrior }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_greysteel }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_fireball }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_hardstone }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_breakspear }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_oakenfist }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_greatheart }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_ironheart }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_neveryield }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_greycloak }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_longspear }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_shieldbreaker }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_shieldsmasher }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_thunderbolt }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_steelskin }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_woe }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_morningstar }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_oakenshield }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_blacksword }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_widowmaker }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_bloodborn }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_starfire }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_windrider }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_swiftspur }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_battleborn }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_swordbiter }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_painter }
				}
			}
			50 = { #Monstrous Nicknames
				trigger = {
					OR = {
						martial >= 14
						prowess >= 20
					}
					OR = {
						has_trait = strong
						has_trait = physique_good
						has_trait = giant
						has_trait = athletic
					}
					OR = {
						has_trait = sadistic
						has_trait = callous
						has_trait = wrathful
						has_trait = impatient
						has_trait = vengeful
					}
				}
				random_list = {
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_awful }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_brute }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_beast }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_hard }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_butcher }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_demon }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_monster }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_slaughterer }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_fiend }
				}
			}
			50 = { #Good Martial
				trigger = {
					martial >= 20
				}
				random_list = {
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_anvil }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_tactician }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_trebuchet }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_warlord }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_battlemaster }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_stone }
				}
			}
			50 = { #Good Diplo
				trigger = {
					diplomacy >= 18
					NOT = { has_trait = callous }
					NOT = { has_trait = rude }
					NOT = { has_trait = wrathful }
				}
				random_list = {
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_silvertongue }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_affable }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_jovial }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_jolly }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_merry }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_eloquent }
				}
			}
			50 = { #Good Learning
				trigger = {
					learning >= 18
				}
				random_list = {
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_reader }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_learned }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_scholar }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_scribe }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_lettered }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_erudite }
				}
			}
			50 = { #Good Intrigue
				trigger = {
					intrigue >= 18
				}
				random_list = {
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_shadow }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_dagger }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_whisperer }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_wily }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_fox }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_spider }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_cunning }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_moonshadow }
				}
			}
			50 = { #Good Stewardship
				trigger = {
					stewardship >= 18
				}
				random_list = {
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_golden }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_gold_hands }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_brilliant }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_exact }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_administrator }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_treasurer }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_pennylover }
				}
			}
			50 = { #Attractive Men
				trigger = {
					is_female = no
					has_trait = beauty_good
				}
				random_list = {
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_handsome }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_brightsmile }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_splendid }
				}
			}
			50 = { #Attractive Women
				trigger = {
					is_female = yes
					has_trait = beauty_good
				}
				random_list = {
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_fair }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_pretty } #pretty pia :)
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_beautiful }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_beauty }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_comely }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_easy_eyes }
				}
			}
			50 = { #Ugly Nicknames
				trigger = {
					has_trait = beauty_bad
				}
				random_list = {
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_ugly }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_homely }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_hideous }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_grotesque }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_beauty_ironic }
				}
			}
			50 = { #Giant Nicknames
				trigger = {
					NOT = {
						has_trait = dwarf
					}
					OR = {
						has_trait = strong
						has_trait = giant
					}
					has_trait = physique_good
					prowess >= 25
				}
				random_list = {
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_mountain }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_titan }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_mighty }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_giant }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_bonebreaker }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_minotaur }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_thunderhead }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_rampage }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_goliath }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_small_ironic }
				}
			}
			50 = { #Drunk Nicknames
				trigger = {
					has_trait = drunkard
				}
				random_list = {
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_sot }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_drunken }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_fermented }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_souse }
				}
			}
			50 = { #Cold-hearted nicknames
				trigger = {
					OR = {
						has_trait = callous
						has_trait = vengeful
					}
					NOT = {
						has_trait = compassionate
						has_trait = forgiving
					}
				}
				random_list = {
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_ruthless }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_merciless }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_heartless }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_stoneheart }
				}
			}
			50 = { #Sadistic Nicknames
				trigger = {
					has_trait = sadistic
					OR = {
						has_trait = wrathful
						has_trait = vengeful
						has_trait = torturer
						has_trait = arbitrary
					}
					NOT = { has_trait = just }
				}
				random_list = {
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_tormentor }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_mutilator }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_depraved }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_monster }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_cruel }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_terrible }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_monstrous }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_weeper }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_barber }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_redhand }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_redarm }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_twisted }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_soulless }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_red_smile }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_tickler }
				}
			}
			50 = { #Brave Nicknames
				trigger = {
					has_trait = brave
					prowess >= 20
				}
				random_list = {
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_brave }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_fearless }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_bold }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_daring }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_tenacious }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_resolute }
				}
			}
			50 = { #Gallant Nicknames
				trigger = {
					ai_honor >= 50
					prowess >= 20
				}
				random_list = {
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_gallant }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_valiant }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_mettle }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_stalwart }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_silverspur }
				}
			}
			50 = { #Strong Nicknames
				trigger = {
					strong_nickname_trigger = yes
					prowess >= 20
				}
				random_list = {
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_strong }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_bull }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_brawny }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_robust }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_hearty }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_durable }
				}
			}
			50 = { #Wild Nicknames
				trigger = {
					OR = {
						has_trait = wrathful
						has_trait = impatient
					}
					has_trait = brave
				}
				random_list = {
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_wild }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_rash }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_fierce }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_feral }
				}
			}
			50 = { #Arrogant Nicknames
				trigger = {
					has_trait = arrogant
				}
				random_list = {
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_arrogant }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_haughty }
				}
			}
			50 = { #Stubborn Nicknames
				trigger = {
					has_trait = stubborn
				}
				random_list = {
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_mule }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_defiant }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_inflexible }
				}
			}
			50 = { #Grim Nicknames
				trigger = {
					ai_sociability < 25
					calc_true_if = {
						amount >= 2
						has_trait = cynical
						has_trait = callous
						has_trait = arrogant
						has_trait = vengeful
						has_trait = sadistic
						has_trait = stubborn
						has_trait = depressed_1
					}
				}
				random_list = {
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_grim }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_sour }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_morbid }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_unsmiling }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_grave }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_stoic }
				}
			}
			50 = { #Clubfoot Nicknames
				trigger = {
					has_trait = clubfooted
				}
				random_list = {
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_clubfoot }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_lame }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_limp }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_limper }
				}
			}
			50 = { #Disfigured Nicknames
				trigger = {
					OR = {
						has_trait = disfigured
						has_trait = crippled
						has_trait = maimed
						calc_true_if = {
							amount >= 2

							has_trait = scarred
							has_trait = one_legged
							has_trait = one_eyed
						}
					}
				}
				random_list = {
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_ruin }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_ruined }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_twisted }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_broken }
				}
			}
			50 = { #Scary Eater Person Nicknames
				trigger = {
					OR = {
						has_trait = gluttonous
						has_trait = cannibal
					}
					prowess >= 25
				}
				random_list = {
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_ironguts }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_maneater }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_paunch }
				}
			}
			50 = {
				trigger = {
					has_trait = lustful
					NOT = { has_trait = just }
					ai_compassion <= high_negative_compassion
					is_female = no
				}
				random_list = {
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_guest }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_maidensbane }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_whoresbane }
				}
			}
			50 = { #Unusual Proclivities Nicknames
				trigger = {
					has_trait = lustful
					OR = {
						has_trait = lunatic

					}
				}
				random_list = {
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_sheep_lover }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_corpse_licker }
				}
			}
			50 = { #Dark Magic Nicknames
				trigger = {
					has_trait = lifestyle_mystic
					OR = {
						has_trait = sadistic
						has_trait = callous
						has_trait = lunatic
						has_trait = possessed
						has_trait = arbitrary
						has_trait = cannibal
					}
				}
				random_list = {

					}
					1 = {
						trigger = { is_female = yes }

			50 = { #Scarred Nicknames
				trigger = {

				}
				random_list = {

					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_scarred }

				}
			}
			50 = { #Unusual Nicknames
				trigger = {
					OR = {
						has_trait = eccentric
						AND = {
							has_sexuality = homosexual
							is_female = no
						}
					}
				}
				random_list = {
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_queer }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_peculiar }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_odd }

			}
			50 = { #Gardener Nicknames
				trigger = {

			50 = { #Poetic Nicknames
				trigger = {
					has_trait = poet
				}
				random_list = {
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_mummer }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_poet }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_bard }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_songbird }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_singer }
				}
			}
			50 = {
				trigger = {
					is_agot_knight_trigger = yes
					NOT = {
						faith = { has_doctrine = tenet_knighthood }
					}
				}
				give_nickname = nick_the_knight
			}
			50 = { #Dreamer Nicknames
				trigger = {
					OR = {
						has_trait = greensight
						has_trait = dragon_dreams
					}
				}

					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_tall_ironic } #irony
				}
			}
			50 = { #Silver-Haired but not Valyrian Nicknames

							has_cultural_pillar = heritage_valyrian
						}
					}
					OR = {

				}

				}
			}

				}
				random_list = {
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_crow }

					1 = { give_nickname = nick_coldhands }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_frostbitten }
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_slushboots }
					1 = {

							prowess >= 20
						}
						give_nickname = nick_snarkslayer
					}
					1 = {
						trigger = {
							prowess >= 20
						}

					}

							}

							has_trait = lustful

				}
				random_list = {
					1 = { give_nickname = nick_the_white }

					}
				}
			}

# Lions - Lannister/Reyne/Osgrey/Grandison
agot_nicknames.0001 = {
	type = character_event
	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		has_any_nickname = no

			dynasty ?= dynasty:dynn_Lannister
			dynasty ?= dynasty:dynn_Reyne
			dynasty ?= dynasty:dynn_Osgrey
			dynasty ?= dynasty:dynn_Grandison
		}
	}

	option = {
		random_list = {
			1 = {}
			5 = {
				trigger = { black_nickname_trigger = yes NOT = { has_global_variable = assigned_nick_the_black_lion } }

				give_nickname = nick_the_black_lion set_global_variable = { name = assigned_nick_the_black_lion value = yes years = 100 }

# Spears - Martell/Stackspear/Moore/Slynt

	type = character_event
	hidden = yes

		has_any_nickname = no
		OR = {
			dynasty ?= dynasty:dynn_Martell
			dynasty ?= dynasty:dynn_Stackspear
			dynasty ?= dynasty:dynn_Moore
			dynasty ?= dynasty:dynn_Slynt
		}
	}

#Oak - Oakheart

#Merman - Manderly

agot_nicknames.0024 = {
	type = character_event
	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		has_any_nickname = no
		dynasty ?= dynasty:dynn_Manderly
	}

	option = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_female = no
			}
			random_list = {
			1 = {} #Fallback
				5 = {
					trigger = { black_nickname_trigger = yes }

						has_trait = nightswatch

		}
	}

	option = {

			1 = {} #Fallback

#Horns - Goodbrother
